All information in the news release is furnished but not filed.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:3pt;margin-top:9pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:700;line-height:110%">Non-GAAP Financial Information</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:5pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">In the attached news release Accenture discloses the following non-GAAP financial measures:</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.85pt">Free cash flow (defined as operating cash flow net of property and equipment additions). Accenture&#8217;s management believes that this information provides meaningful additional information regarding the company&#8217;s liquidity.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.85pt">Percentage changes in revenues and bookings on a local currency basis. Financial results in local currency are calculated by restating current period activity into U.S. dollars using the comparable prior year period&#8217;s foreign currency exchange rates. This approach is used for all results where the functional currency is not the U.S. dollar. Accenture&#8217;s management believes that information regarding changes in its revenues and bookings that excludes the effect of fluctuations in foreign currency exchange rates facilitates meaningful comparison of its revenues.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:18pt;text-indent:-18pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#8226;</span><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.85pt">Adjusted financial measures excluding the impact of business optimization costs, with adjusted earnings per share and adjusted effective tax rate outlook additionally excluding an anticipated investment gain. Accenture&#8217;s management believes that information regarding the effect of the business optimization costs and the investment gain facilitates an understanding as to the impact of these items and the company&#8217;s performance in comparison to the prior period.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt;margin-top:9pt"><span style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Reconciliations of these non-GAAP financial measures to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP are included in the news release. While Accenture&#8217;s management believes that this non-GAAP financial information is useful in evaluating Accenture&#8217;s operations, this information should be considered as supplemental in nature and not as a substitute for the related financial information prepared in accordance with GAAP.</span></div><div style="margin-bottom:34pt;margin-top:9pt"><span><br/></span></div><div adjusted operating margin is 13.8%, an expansion of 10 basis points --</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt;text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">-- Company declares quarterly cash dividend of $1.12 per share, up 15% from a year ago -- </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt;text-align:center"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">-- Accenture updates business outlook</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:7.15pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;position:relative;top:-3.85pt;vertical-align:baseline">2</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%"> for fiscal 2023&#59; now expects full-year revenue growth of 8% to 10% in local currency and foreign-exchange impact of negative 4.5%&#59; GAAP operating margin of 14.1% to 14.3%&#59; adjusted operating margin of 15.3% to 15.5%&#59; GAAP EPS of $10.84 to $11.06&#59; adjusted EPS of $11.41 to $11.63&#59; increases operating cash flow range to $8.7 billion to $9.2 billion from $8.5 billion to $9.0 billion&#59; and increases free cash flow range to $8.0 billion to $8.5 billion from $7.7 billion to $8.2 billion -- </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">NEW YORK&#59; March&#160;23, 2023 &#8212; Accenture (NYSE&#58; ACN) reported financial results for the second quarter of fiscal 2023, ended February&#160;28, 2023, with revenues of $15.8 billion, an increase of 5% in U.S. dollars and 9% in local currency over the same period last year. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">GAAP operating income was $1.94 billion, compared to $2.06 billion for the second quarter last year, and operating margin was 12.3% compared to 13.7% for the second quarter last year. Adjusted operating margin was 13.8%, an expansion of 10 basis points from the second quarter of fiscal 2022.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">GAAP diluted earnings per share were $2.39, compared to $2.54 for the second quarter last year. Adjusted EPS were $2.69, an increase of 6% from the second quarter of fiscal 2022.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">New bookings for the quarter were a record $22.1 billion, with consulting bookings of $10.7 billion and managed services bookings of $11.4 billion.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:28pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Julie Sweet, chair and CEO, Accenture, said, &#8220;Our strong financial results this quarter again demonstrate that our ability to bring together industry, functional and technology expertise as well as managed services continues to differentiate us with our clients. Our record bookings reflect the confidence and trust that our clients have in us to create value and help them transform at speed. We are also taking steps to lower our costs in fiscal year 2024 and beyond while continuing to invest in our business and our people to capture the significant growth opportunities ahead.&#8221;</font></div><div><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:5.85pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;position:relative;top:-3.15pt;vertical-align:baseline">1</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:9pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Adjusted financial measures presented in this release are non-GAAP financial measures that exclude the impact of business optimization costs, as further described in this release.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:9pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:5.85pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;position:relative;top:-3.15pt;vertical-align:baseline">2</font><font related to our investment in Duck Creek Technologies expected to be recorded in the first half of calendar year 2023.</font></div><div style="height:72pt;position:relative;width:100%"><div style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Revenues for the second quarter of fiscal 2023 were $15.81 billion, compared with $15.05 billion for the second quarter of fiscal 2022, an increase of 5% in U.S. dollars and 9% in local currency. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">Revenues for the quarter reflect a foreign-exchange impact of approximately negative 4% compared with the negative 5% impact previously assumed. Adjusting for the actual foreign-exchange impact, the company&#8217;s guided range for quarterly revenues was approximately $15.35 billion to $15.90 billion. Accenture&#8217;s second quarter fiscal 2023 revenues were at the top of this adjusted range.</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">Consulting revenues for the quarter were $8.28 billion, a decrease of 1% in U.S. dollars and an increase of 4% in local currency compared with the second quarter of fiscal 2022. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">Managed Services revenues were $7.54 billion, an increase of 12% in U.S. dollars and 16% in local currency compared with the second quarter of fiscal 2022. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:8pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">During the second quarter of fiscal 2023, Accenture initiated actions to streamline operations, transform non-billable corporate functions and consolidate office space to reduce costs. The company recorded $244 million in business optimization costs during the second quarter and expects to record total costs of approximately $1.5 billion through fiscal 2024. Accenture estimates $1.2 billion for severance and $300 million for consolidation of office space, with approximately $800 million expected in fiscal 2023 and $700 million in fiscal 2024. </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">GAAP diluted EPS for the quarter were $2.39 compared with $2.54 for the second quarter of fiscal 2022. Adjusted EPS were $2.69, an increase of 6% from the second quarter of fiscal 2022. The $0.15 increase in EPS on an adjusted basis reflects&#58;</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">a $0.16&#160;increase from higher revenue and operating results&#59; </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">a $0.02 increase from lower share count&#59; and</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">a $0.02 increase from higher non-operating income&#59; </font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">      partially offset by</font></div><div style="margin-bottom:7pt;margin-top:5pt;padding-left:36pt;text-indent:-18pt"><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%">&#9642;</font><font style="color:#000000;font-family:'Arial',sans-serif;font-size:11pt;font-weight:400;line-height:120%;padding-left:14.11pt">a $0.04&#160;decrease from a higher effective tax rate&#59; e.removeAttribute('id');a.parentNode.appendChild(e)}}
if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
e.style.display=d;if(a.textContent){a.textContent=p+a.textContent.substring(1)}else{a.innerText=p+a.innerText.substring(1)}}}
